She always made sure I was aware of any activities going on at the resort and invited me to make use of the amenities (spa, cocktail hour, etc.).

The landscaping was also very elegant, with interesting trees and plants all around.  I appreciated the very serene and pleasant environment as a background for relaxation.

Quiet location away from tourist hub:  There aren't too many attractions around nor outside visitors, which provides a calm and private place for those who don't want to be in the "middle of it all." 

Thank you for a lovely experience!

name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted May 10, 2024
msg:About the experience of staying at Capella Hotel:
This time I came to Sanya and booked three hotels, namely Rosewood, Mandarin Oriental and Capella. The price of Capella is actually the most expensive, so I thought the service and environment should be the best, but after checking in, I was surprised to find that it was so disappointing.
First of all, in terms of service, (objective review), the good thing is that flowers and honeymoon cakes were sent with a sense of ceremony when checking in. I will also describe the bad things one by one. First of all, the room that costs more than 3,000 yuan a night did not have a Dyson hair dryer. I had to call the guest room phone to send one; secondly, the hotel is very large, but there are very few shuttle buses, and they come very slowly even if I call them. Mandarin Oriental does a better job in this regard; finally, I feel that the service staff has a weak sense of service. In the morning, he knocked on the door and asked me if I could clean the room. I said it would be later, and he asked when it could be cleaned (I have stayed in many five-star hotels and have never seen such service staff.) When I ate, I asked for two glasses of iced Americano, but no one came after waiting for a long time. I asked again and they hurried to do it. When checking out, my husband and I were carrying heavy luggage, and a waiter followed us and played with his phone all the way without asking to come over to help.
The second is the environment and breakfast. Capella has its own characteristics in both the garden and the room, without losing the sense of design. The Chinese garden a**osphere is reflected in all aspects, but there are many small insects flying in the elevator at night, which has never appeared in other hotels! The breakfast is really great, richer and more attentive than other hotels.
In summary, I heard that Capella is the ceiling of Sanya hotels, but it is really disappointing. The service staff at the beach or at the door are sometimes on duty and sometimes not. The light switches in the room are not clearly marked. There is not even sugar-free cola in the refrigerator. It is not as good as the magnificent and Oriental Mandarin, which are one or two thousand cheaper than him. I hope the hotel can recognize its own positioning. As for me, I will not consider staying here next time I come to Sanya.

The characteristics are EDITION (close to duty-free shops and many in-person projects), Magnificent (only the swimming pool is the highlight), and Park Hyatt (ocean view room has a good view). However, my personal favorite is Mandarin Oriental, with its accumulated heritage and The service is unparalleled, but the facilities are a bit old and the room has a musty smell.
Capella is located in Tufu Bay, Lingshui, which is still some distance away from Haitang Bay. A housekeeper named Eda is very enthusiastic and will accompany and share various activities and services of the hotel.
There are only farmhouses in the surrounding area, and it takes 20 minutes to drive to the duty-free city CDF. It is also difficult to take out food in the hotel. The Thai food in the hotel restaurant Babeibabei is of good quality, but it is expensive. The two of them spent more than 1,600. There are not many varieties of breakfast, but the quality is okay.
There is a happy hour with free afternoon tea, which tastes good.
The hotel room is very nice, with a large area and exquisite online decoration. The minibar has a good level of free non-alcoholic drinks and fruits. The balcony has a little sea view, which is relatively far away.
The overall environment of the hotel is also very good, with high-level greening and architecture. The spa center is well-equipped and the igloo service is also good. It is very fast to go to the pool and beach with a battery car. The swimming pool design is good. Because there are not many guests, most areas of the hotel are relatively quiet and have a resort feel.

We have experienced: coconut leaf weaving, water mist magic beads, stone painting, etc. There is also a small chef activity (making small biscuits or pizza, etc.) for a fee of 188/time
The full-time living room bar provides unlimited free non-alcoholic soft drinks and fruits from 11:00-18:00.
Every day from 15:00 to 16:00 Silk Road Restaurant has free afternoon tea (the types are basically fixed)
In the past few days, I have experienced two restaurants of Capella - Lanting Chinese Restaurant and Western Restaurant. The overall feeling is that Chinese food is more to our appetite. There is also a set meal of 888 yuan on Father's Day. The dishes are large and the cooking is exquisite.
All the staff of Capella are warm and professional in service, and it really feels like home here.
The soft power of the hotel's humanistic services is superb, and the hardware facilities are also very good.
The spa and gym are very recommended, there are few people and quiet, so you can relax.
Looking forward to meeting here next time.

Give you a thumbs up!

"Morning Ritual" at 8:30 in the morning - Water Tai Chi
Super long breakfast buffet: until 11 am, you can eat brunch directly! It is recommended to have a bowl of local characteristic Hainan Baoluo noodles!
Free afternoon snacks at 3-4 p.m., you only need to be seated, and the staff will serve you rich snacks~
Into the night ceremony from 6 to 7 in the evening - tasting different cocktails every day, and there are also non-alcoholic cocktails for friends who don't drink~
As for the restaurant, I checked in at The Dempsey Western Restaurant in the hotel, booked an outdoor seat, watched the beautiful scenery, and had dinner. It was really wonderful.
The hotel's main swimming pool is super fun, I had a lot of fun, lol~
The hotel exclusively enjoys a beach. The sand on the beach is very fine and clean. It is soft and comfortable when you step on it~

Service: There is nothing to say about the overall service. Environment: The hotel has a lot of green plants in general. During the two days I went there, I saw staff disinfecting mosquitoes, so my "mosquito-sucking physique" was not bitten at all in the hotel! This feels really great!

Finally, I would like to say that Capella's coconut water is really delicious~thanks to my cultural travel officer Anna!

msg:Capella is the hotel that my family and I have always wanted to check in. In order to make the hotel develop better, here is an open and honest review.
1. The core product, the room, has booked a basic room type, and can directly upgrade to a studio suite at the front desk. Impressive points for first-time customers. There are a few free snacks and drinks in the room. The most comfortable thing is the bedding, which is the most comfortable I have ever slept on. I especially like the towels and bath towels in the bathroom, which are absorbent and comfortable. Nice!
2. For breakfast, all meals are taken by the waiter. Ruisby is economical and clean. I personally like it very much and this is the first time I have experienced it. I just don't know if the customers will queue up when there are many times. Very good!
3. Room service, in the coldest place in Hainan, when I arrived at the store because of cold diarrhea, I delivered food twice‚ûïreceived food, cleaned once, three times‚ûïquilt and quilt cover, the waiter took the trouble to satisfy them one by one. not expensive. But very warm. Fried chicken like!
Here are the points to complain about:
4. As a loyal Marriott Platinum member for many years, I rarely stay in other hotels, so the room type is upgraded to a studio room. For any Marriott hotel that stays casually, it is given priority to upgrade to a villa or suite, and the check-in time is not limited, and the check-out time is always For me at 16 o'clock, Capella is a cold face to me. Even if I checked into Capella at 4:30, I was asked to leave the hotel at 12:00 the next day. After thick-skinned negotiations ‚ûï shameless late check-out, I managed to leave the room at 13:45, feeling insulted!
Suggestion: Can guests who check in late be able to delay generously, and don't let the waiter's speech skills give me the feeling that it is a charity for me.
5. The waiter promised to have a departure gift, but the check out didn't know if it was because we were late. We didn't mention it at all, and we didn't really have the nerve to speak up, so we left.
Suggestion: Don't promise if you can't do it, I don't need gifts, but don't say anything, I thank you, you are gone...
6. Lunch: Capella is located in a remote location, surrounded by original village houses and orchards. There are no restaurants and takeaways, so you can only eat here. Among the grilled wings on the menu, the ones that come up are fried wings, which are completely inconsistent with the pictures and texts; the coconut soup and the example soup are shi people, and the steak in the middle of the beef burger is very salty and has a fishy smell; the service consciousness of the waiters is not bad, and they know me Each dish was withdrawn after only a sip. I hurried to find the manager to apologize. The attitude was very good, but I didn't want to accept it. It is acceptable for one dish to be bad, and there are problems with each one. The hotel should consider changing the chef team.
Suggestion: People nowadays are healthy and healthy. If there is fried food on the menu, I will not order it. The discrepancy between the pictures and the text is a low-level mistake of elementary school students. Capella will not be short of money to buy wings. The dishes are so salty, tell me that because of the long cooking time, this is not an attitude of admitting mistakes, my aunt's cooking is better than Chef Capella's.
7. I experienced the biggest spa in history and the most difficult to make an appoin**ent. On the first night, I made an appoin**ent for two people at the spa and was told that I could only be one person, so my family and I had to be separated. The waiter said that I got off work at 10 o'clock, so I don't mind coming later. I replied that as long as there are two people, any night is fine. As a result, the semi-finals of the World Cup ended and ignored us. I went the next morning and said that the door would not open until twelve o‚Äôclock (I didn‚Äôt know that when I arrived in Qatar, there were no two employees who went to work a day. I didn‚Äôt want to work overtime for how much money I paid!) Thinking that I had to finish lunch and go to the spa, the front desk urged me to leave Room, I tried to send money to Capella but was rejected many times. As far as this service is concerned, it is worthy of being a hotel controlled by a central enterprise, and it is not short of money!

Finally, to sum up, based on my experience of 300 days of business trips, it is already very difficult for hotels to make profits from guest rooms. They will find secondary consumption points through catering‚ûïleisure mode. I personally support this. The hotel makes money, the employees are good, and the employees are satisfied. Will serve customers better. But your product must be hardcore enough to attract customers. The hardware part, because it is a new hotel, so the hardware is not a problem. Because it is a parent-child trip, I pay more attention to the parent-child facilities part. Capella does a very good job in this part. It has three parks for children to play. The younger ones can go to the kids club, the older ones can go to the adventure park, and the younger ones can go to the water park. Both the kids club and the adventure park are divided into indoor and outdoor areas. It will be open until 6 o'clock if it doesn't rain, and the staff said it will be extended to 8 o'clock if it rains. Kids club has awnings in the sand digging area and slide area to prevent children from being exposed to the sun. This is really intimate and friendly. Most of the hotel‚Äôs outdoor children‚Äôs playgrounds do not take this into consideration. Moreover, the indoor facilities are not as good-looking as many hotels, but the playability is not good. In places where I can't take pictures, I saw that they also have badminton, table tennis, and various chess sets that can be used. Really recommend a parent-child trip to experience.

Service part: It should be said that it is the ceiling of Sanya hotel so far. Most of the staff will try their best to assist hotel guests and make you feel at home. For example, catching crabs on the beach, here every night, and not one or two employees take a group of people, but one-to-one service, it is a pity that I did not remember the name of the little girl who took us to dig crabs that day. It's really hard work!

Very enthusiastic to take the children to play cars, play chess, play with water guns, and pick coconuts. Very patient. It can be compared to the GO of beautiful club med. I heard that there are custody services for winter and summer vacations. The kids hope to see Uncle Tony again when that time comes! The elder sister in the children's playground (forgot to ask for the name) is also very active and enthusiastic to play with the children. This is the warmth I can't experience in other hotels. This makes Capella a hotel like no other.

As for my cultural and tourism officer, Helen, I also want to be praised by name. She tried her best to solve my problems in various aspects of the accommodation, such as mosquito elimination, restaurant reservations, sanitary equipment maintenance, and so on.

Another suggestion is that the octopus in the penultimate picture is a flushing facility next to the kids club sand pit. It is recommended to repair and resume use, because after playing in the sand pit, it needs to be flushed and cleaned. The last one is a water supply facility in the bunkers. The bunkers abroad have water. The original intention was that children with running water could pile sand, but dry sand could not make a castle. Of course, it may increase management difficulties when there is water, so this function is currently disabled, and only the staff can use it when washing toys. What a pity!

Finally, I really recommend parents and children to experience Capella. When the epidemic slows down, I also hope to experience Capella hotels in other countries!

Although the hotel is expensive, it is highly recommended to experience it. During the entire stay, there will be cultural and tourism officials on WeChat. If you need to book an event restaurant or have questions, you can directly contact us. Our cultural and tourism officer Effy is very enthusiastic, answering all questions, with a friendly attitude and must be praised. In addition, travel is not very convenient, so you must drive by yourself.
